However, the jetpack overheats quickly, and the Pathfinder is limited in the amount of jumps that he can make in a period of time. Completing a jump kicks up a great deal of dust, almost completely cloaking the Pathfinder from sight for a short time.<n/><n/>Level 2 -- 300 damage, 8 range, AOE 3.5, grants 85% evasion for 1.5 seconds
